		}

			country_event = { id=stalliongrad_start.62 }
		}
	}

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event stalliongrad_start.67" }
	title = stalliongrad_start.67.t
	desc = stalliongrad_start.67.d
	picture = GFX_event_stg_red_army

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = stalliongrad_start.67.a
		activate_decision = STG_sinister_coup
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = STG_sinnie_coup_flag
			country_event = { id=stalliongrad_start.69 days = 3 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {				#Sinister win his coup without battle
	id = stalliongrad_start.74
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event stalliongrad_start.74" }
	title = stalliongrad_start.74.t
	desc = stalliongrad_start.74.d
	picture = GFX_event_stg_red_army

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = stalliongrad_start.74.a
		retire_country_leader = yes
		promote_character = STG_sinister_serov
		load_focus_tree = stalliongrad_sinne
		clr_country_flag = STG_avaliable_party_mechainc
		remove_dynamic_modifier = {
			modifier = STG_left_center_right_buffs
		}
		STG_caramelka_sladkaya = {
			remove_advisor_role = { slot = political_advisor }
		}
		STG_dark_wing = {
			remove_advisor_role = { slot = political_advisor }
		}
		STG_vasiliy_wheatin = {
			remove_advisor_role = { slot = political_advisor }
		}
		STG_gold_muffin = {
			remove_advisor_role = { slot = political_advisor }
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			STG_alevtina_qubysheva = {
				remove_advisor_role = { slot = political_advisor }
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communism
			popularity = -0.4
		}
		set_country_flag = STG_alevtina_qubysheva_fired
		STG_alexandra_mistina = {
			remove_advisor_role = { slot = political_advisor }
			remove_unit_leader_role = yes
		}
		STG_amber_flyagin = {
			remove_advisor_role = { slot = political_advisor }
			remove_unit_leader_role = yes

		}
	}
}

country_event = {			#Blood on the streets and squares of Stalliongrad
	id = stalliongrad_start.84
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event stalliongrad_start.84" }
	title = stalliongrad_start.84.t
	desc = stalliongrad_start.84.d
	picture = GFX_event_stg_red_army

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = stalliongrad_start.84.a
		random_list = {
			1 = {
				modifier = {
					add = STG_left_opposition_support
				}
				modifier = {
					has_country_flag = STG_sinnie_coup_flag_0
					add = 5
				}
				modifier = {
					has_country_flag = STG_sinnie_coup_flag_1
					add = 5
				}
				modifier = {
					has_country_flag = STG_sinnie_coup_flag_2
					add = 5
				}
				modifier = {
					has_country_flag = STG_sinnie_coup_flag_3
					add = 5
				}
				add_manpower = -231
				country_event = { id=stalliongrad_start.89 days = 5 }
				add_to_variable = { STG_main_party_support = -10 tooltip = STG_get_main_oppose_value_tt }
				add_to_variable = { STG_left_opposition_support = 20 tooltip = STG_get_left_oppose_value_tt }
				add_to_variable = { STG_right_opposition_support = -10 tooltip = STG_get_right_oppose_value_tt }
				STG_check_party_variables = yes
				hidden_effect = {
					country_event = { id=stalliongrad_start.88 days = 3 }
				}
			}
			1 = {
				modifier = {
					add = STG_right_opposition_support
				}
				modifier = {
					has_country_flag = STG_sladkova_prepares_flag_0
					add = 5
				}
				modifier = {
					has_country_flag = STG_sladkova_prepares_flag_1
					add = 5
				}
				modifier = {
					has_country_flag = STG_sladkova_prepares_flag_2
					add = 5
				}
				modifier = {
					has_country_flag = STG_sladkova_prepares_flag_3
					add = 5
				}
				add_manpower = -231
				country_event = { id=stalliongrad_start.90 days = 5 }
				add_to_variable = { STG_main_party_support = -10 tooltip = STG_get_main_oppose_value_tt }
				add_to_variable = { STG_left_opposition_support = -10 tooltip = STG_get_left_oppose_value_tt }
				add_to_variable = { STG_right_opposition_support = 20 tooltip = STG_get_right_oppose_value_tt }
				STG_check_party_variables = yes
				hidden_effect = {
					country_event = { id=stalliongrad_start.88 days = 3 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

country_event = {
	id = stalliongrad_start.91
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event stalliongrad_start.91" }
	title = stalliongrad_start.91.t
	desc = stalliongrad_start.91.d
	picture = GFX_event_stg_red_army

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = stalliongrad_start.91.a		
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = STG_production_center_plan
			days = 90
		}
		add_to_variable = { STG_main_party_support = 4 tooltip = STG_get_main_oppose_value_tt }
		add_to_variable = { STG_left_opposition_support = -2 tooltip = STG_get_left_oppose_value_tt }
		add_to_variable = { STG_right_opposition_support = -2 tooltip = STG_get_right_oppose_value_tt }
		STG_check_party_variables = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = stalliongrad_start.91.b
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = STG_production_rightist_plan
			days = 90
		}
		add_to_variable = { STG_main_party_support = -2 tooltip = STG_get_main_oppose_value_tt }
		add_to_variable = { STG_left_opposition_support = -2 tooltip = STG_get_left_oppose_value_tt }

	title = stalliongrad_propaganda_campaign_events.2.t

		hidden_effect = {

				days = 180
			}
			#RESET PROPAGANDA CAMPAIGN
			set_rule = { can_send_volunteers = yes }

			set_variable = { STG_propaganda_campaign_to_remove = 25 }
			STG_reset_propaganda_campaign_slot_effect = yes
		}
	}

	option = { #OK
		name = stalliongrad_propaganda_campaign_events.2.a

		effect_tooltip = {
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = STG_broken_peace_dreams_attacker
				days = 180
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # The big demands-list event!
	id = stalliongrad_vasily.7
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event stalliongrad_vasily.7" }
	title = stalliongrad_vasily.7.t
	desc = stalliongrad_vasily.7.d
	picture = GFX_event_stg_red_army

	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_variable = STG_asking_times } }
				set_variable = { STG_asking_times = 1 }
			}
			else = {
				add_to_variable = { STG_asking_times = 1 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # lift embargo
		name = stalliongrad_vasily.7.a
		set_country_flag = STG_asks_for_lvl1
		EQS = {
			country_event = {
				id = stalliongrad_vasily.8
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # as above, plus territory after war
		name = stalliongrad_vasily.7.b
		set_country_flag = STG_asks_for_lvl2
		EQS = {
			country_event = {
				id = stalliongrad_vasily.8
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # as above, but territory immediately
		name = stalliongrad_vasily.7.c
		set_country_flag = STG_asks_for_lvl3
		EQS = {
			country_event = {
				id = stalliongrad_vasily.8
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # as above, plus EQS lifts cores, and NAP with EQS
		name = stalliongrad_vasily.7.e
		set_country_flag = STG_asks_for_lvl4
		EQS = {
			country_event = {
				id = stalliongrad_vasily.8
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

	}

				has_country_flag = STG_asks_for_lvl3

		}
	}

	option = { # Fine, take it

				has_country_flag = STG_asks_for_lvl1	
			}
		}

		set_global_flag = EQS_STG_deal_lvl1

			base = 10
		}
		STG = {

				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Fine, take it
		trigger = {
			STG = {
				has_country_flag = STG_asks_for_lvl2
			}
		}
		name = stalliongrad_vasily.8.a
		set_global_flag = EQS_STG_deal_lvl2
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				add = 1000
				surrender_progress > 0.10
			}
		}
		STG = {
			country_event = {
				id = stalliongrad_vasily.10
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Fine, take it
		trigger = {
			STG = {
				has_country_flag = STG_asks_for_lvl3
			}
		}
		name = stalliongrad_vasily.8.a
		set_global_flag = EQS_STG_deal_lvl3
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				add = 1000
				surrender_progress > 0.20
			}
		}
		STG = {
			country_event = {
				id = stalliongrad_vasily.10
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Fine, take it
		trigger = {
			STG = {
				has_country_flag = STG_asks_for_lvl4
			}
		}
		name = stalliongrad_vasily.8.a
		set_global_flag = EQS_STG_deal_lvl4
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				add = 1000

			}

country_event = { # STG - EQS refused
	id = stalliongrad_vasily.11
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event stalliongrad_vasily.11" }
	title = stalliongrad_vasily.11.t
	desc = stalliongrad_vasily.11.d
	picture = GFX_event_stg_red_army

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # at least we can try again
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				STG_asking_times < 4
			}
		}
		name = stalliongrad_vasily.11.a
		clr_country_flag = STG_asks_for_lvl1
		clr_country_flag = STG_asks_for_lvl2
		clr_country_flag = STG_asks_for_lvl3
		clr_country_flag = STG_asks_for_lvl4
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = STG_can_ask_EQS
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = STG_can_ask_EQS
		}
	}
	option = { # welp it's over
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				STG_asking_times > 3
			}
		}
		name = stalliongrad_vasily.11.b
		clr_country_flag = STG_asks_for_lvl1
		clr_country_flag = STG_asks_for_lvl2
		clr_country_flag = STG_asks_for_lvl3
		clr_country_flag = STG_asks_for_lvl4
		set_global_flag = STG_EQS_negotiations_failed
	}
	
}

### Sinister's industrial plan events ###

country_event = {
	id = stalliongrad_sinister.10
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event stalliongrad_sinister.10" }
	title = stalliongrad_sinister.10.t
	desc = stalliongrad_sinister.10.d
	picture = GFX_event_stg_red_army

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = stalliongrad_sinister.10.a ##Plan activation
		add_dynamic_modifier = {
			modifier = STG_sinister_industry_modifier
		}
		add_to_variable = { STG_sinister_industry_consumer_goods_factor = 0.6 tooltip = STG_industrial_mechanic_activation_tt } 
		set_country_flag = STG_industrial_plan_activated
		STG = { country_event = { id = stalliongrad_sinister.11 days = 7 } }
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = civilian_economy
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = civilian_economy
				add_idea = STG_sinnie_unique_tot_economic_mobilisation
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = low_economic_mobilisation
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = low_economic_mobilisation
				add_idea = STG_sinnie_unique_tot_economic_mobilisation
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = partial_economic_mobilisation
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = partial_economic_mobilisation
				add_idea = STG_sinnie_unique_tot_economic_mobilisation
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = war_economy
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = war_economy
				add_idea = STG_sinnie_unique_tot_economic_mobilisation
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = tot_economic_mobilisation
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = tot_economic_mobilisation
				add_idea = STG_sinnie_unique_tot_economic_mobilisation
			}
		}
		# this should never happen but i'm paranoid
		else = {
			add_ideas = STG_sinnie_unique_tot_economic_mobilisation
		}

    }
}

	picture = GFX_event_stg_red_army
	fire_only_once = yes

		has_country_flag = STG_sombra_cultists_were_manage_to_excape
		has_war_with_major = yes
		casualties_k > 150
	}

	option = {
		name = stalliongrad_sinister.96.a	
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = STG_execution_for_sombra_cultists }
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = STG_revenge_from_sombra_cultist_idea
				days = 180
			}
			#TODO add hub and infrastructure damage in crystal city
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = STG_prison_for_sombra_cultists }
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = STG_revenge_from_sombra_cultist_idea
				days = 365
			}
			#TODO add hub and infrastructure damage in crystal city and somewhere where will be prison
		}
		else = {
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = STG_revenge_from_sombra_cultist_idea
				days = 365
			}
			add_political_power = -50
			add_stability = -0.025
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = communism
				popularity = -0.075
			}
		}
	}
}

		}
		else = {
			set_country_flag = STG_grom_was_wounded
		}
		set_country_flag = STG_postECW_hunt_solarists_excaped_flag
	}
}

	}

#fires in the scope of the country to be annexed/puppeted by STG
country_event = {
	id = stalliongrad_old.148
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event stalliongrad_old.148"}
	title = stalliongrad_old.148.t
	desc = stalliongrad_old.148.d
	picture = GFX_event_stg_pairlament



	is_triggered_only = yes

	#okay we gonna die
	option = {
		name = stalliongrad_old.148.a
		hidden_effect = {
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				if = {
					limit = { is_eqs_civil_war_tag = yes is_ai = yes }
					FROM = { annex_country = { target = PREV transfer_troops = yes } }
				}
				else = {
					end_puppet_this = yes
					hidden_effect = {
						get_current_government_type = yes
					}
					FROM = { puppet = PREV }
					hidden_effect = {
						restore_previous_government_type = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GAME_OVER_TT
		FROM = {
			annex_country = { target = ROOT transfer_troops = yes }
			country_event = { id = stalliongrad_old.149 days = 1 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
	}

	#okay we gonna be puppet
	option = {
		trigger = { is_subject = no }
		name = stalliongrad_old.148.b
		hidden_effect = {
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				if = {
					limit = { is_eqs_civil_war_tag = yes is_ai = yes }
					FROM = { annex_country = { target = PREV transfer_troops = yes } }
				}
				else = {
					end_puppet_this = yes
					hidden_effect = {
						get_current_government_type = yes
					}
					FROM = { puppet = PREV }
					hidden_effect = {
						restore_previous_government_type = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			puppet = ROOT
			country_event = { id = stalliongrad_old.149 days = 1 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}

	#nah fuck you fam
	option = {
		name = stalliongrad_old.148.c
		FROM = {
			effect_tooltip = {
				if = {
					limit = { is_subject_of = FROM }
					end_puppet_this = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_in_faction_with = FROM }
					leave_faction = yes
				}
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = ROOT
					modifier = hostility
				}
				create_wargoal = {
					type = annex_everything
					target = ROOT
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = stalliongrad_old.150 days = 1 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
}
